Group Nr.	By the rule of parsimony, we have gathered all proteins sharing the same identified peptides into a single group.

Protein Name	The protein name in the DB.

#		Serial (sequential) number for peptide.
Sequence	Assigned peptide sequence. Periods (".") delimit the sequence for internal peptides.
PTM Site	Location of the post-translational modification (PTM) in the peptide.
		Modification codes: [1] Oxidation (M)
Nr. Scans	The number of MS/MS scans that were matched to this peptide.
Mascot Score	Score given to this peptide/spectrum match by Mascot.
Expectation	The number of matches with equal or better scores that are expected to occur by chance alone.
Isolated Mass	"Mass" in the Orbitrap analyzer.
Delta Mass	Difference between the observed and theoretical masses, in ppm.
Charge State	Inferred ionic state of the peptide.
Matched Ions	Number of matched MS/MS ions, as reported by Mascot. NOTE: Temporarily disabled.
Scan Nr.	MS/MS scan number in the original Xcalibur RAW file.
